class=\"cash-amount\">' + transaction.ReceiveAmount + '</span>';\n            box += '<span class=\"currency\">' + transaction.ReceiveCurrency + '</span>';\n            box += '<span class=\"bottom-text\">As <span class=\"method\">' + transaction.PaymentMode + '</span></span>';\n            box += '</div>';\n            box += '</div>';\n\n            return box;\n\n        }\n\n        // Converts elapsed time for display\n        // If > 1 hour, return null\n        // If not, return back the mins\n        function convertTime(elapsedTime) {\n\n            if (elapsedTime) {\n                var time = elapsedTime.split(':');\n\n                if (time[0] >= 1) {\n                    return null;\n                } else {\n                    return parseInt(time[1], 10);\n                }\n\n            }\n\n        }\n\n        // Append success and failure to promise\n        promise.then(success, failure);\n\n        // Append transaction to the flow\n        function appendTransaction(box, time) {\n            var convertedTime = convertTime(time),\n                timeUnit = 'min',\n                colName = '.right-tracker', // defaults to right column\n                newTransaction = '',\n                oval = '<img class=\"oval-tracker\" src=\"/~/media/images/marketing/icons/tracker-oval.ashx\" alt=\"oval tracker\" />',\n                ovalTop = '',\n                ovalBottom = '',\n                ovalBox = '';\n\n            // If converted time is null, then set default 1 hour\n            if (!convertedTime) {\n                convertedTime = '1';\n                timeUnit = 'hour';\n            }\n\n            // Decide on right or left column\n            // col =\n            if (!col) {\n                colName = '.left-tracker';\n                ovalTop = '';\n                ovalBottom = oval;\n            } else {\n                ovalTop = oval;\n                ovalBottom = '';\n            }\n\n\n            // Oval UI\n            ovalBox += '<div class=\"transaction-tracker-circle\">';\n            ovalBox += ovalTop;\n            ovalBox += '<span class=\"transaction-time-section\">';\n            ovalBox += '<hr class=\"line\" />';\n            ovalBox += '<span class=\"transaction-time\">' + convertedTime + ' ' + timeUnit + '</span>';\n            ovalBox += '</span>';\n            ovalBox += ovalBottom;\n            ovalBox += '</div>';\n\n\n            // Compile New Transaction box\n            newTransaction += '<div class=\"transaction-container\">';\n            newTransaction += box;\n            newTransaction += ovalBox;\n            newTransaction += '</div>';\n\n\n            // Append new transaction to DOM\n            $(colName).append(newTransaction);\n\n            // Switch column flag for next transaction\n            col = !col;\n\n        }\n\n        // Animate tracker for vertical shift\n        function animateTracker() {\n            currentDisplace = currentDisplace + incrementDisplace;\n            $('.left-tracker').animate({ 'top': currentDisplace + 'px' }, 80);\n            $('.right-tracker').animate({ 'top': currentDisplace + 'px' }, 80);\n        }\n\n    });\n\n\n</script>                    <div id=\"content-mktg-green\" class=\"row\">\n                        <div class=\"col-xs-12\">\n                            <div
